  TicTacToe
    #initialize
      assigns an instance variable @board to an array with 9 blank spaces " "
    WIN_COMBINATIONS
      defines a constant WIN_COMBINATIONS with arrays for each win combination
    #display_board
      prints arbitrary arrangements of the board
    #move
      allows "X" player in the top left and "O" in the middle
    #position_taken?
      returns true/false based on position in board
    #valid_move?
      returns true/false based on position
    #turn
      makes valid moves and displays the board (FAILED - 1)
      asks for input again after a failed validation (FAILED - 2)
    #turn_count
      counts occupied positions
    #current_player
      returns the correct player, X, for the third move
    #won?
      returns false for a draw
      returns true for a win
    #full?
      returns true for a draw
      returns false for an in-progress game
    #draw?
      returns true for a draw
      returns false for a won game
      returns false for an in-progress game
    #over?
      returns true for a draw
      returns true for a won game
      returns false for an in-progress game
    #winner
      return X when X won
      returns O when O won
      returns nil when no winner
